[김상훈] [오후 4:53] package chapter15;
/*
String -> Integer 변환해서 출력
Integer->int 변환해서 출력
int -> Integer 변환해서 출력
오토 박싱, 오토 언박싱은 사용하지말고 직접 메소드사용해서 변환

실행결과
Integer1=100
intValue=100
Integer2=100
*/
public class WrapperTest4 {

   public static void main(String[] args) {
      
      String str="100";
      Integer integer1 = Integer.parseInt(str);
      System.out.println("Integer1 : "+integer1);
      int intValue = integer1.intValue();
      System.out.println("intValue : "+intValue);
      Integer integer2=Integer.valueOf(intValue);
      System.out.println("Integer2 : "+integer2);

      
      
   }
   
}

[홍성훈] [오후 4:55] package chapter15;

public class WrapperTest04 {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        
        String str = "100";
        
        // String -> Integer
        Integer integer1 = Integer.valueOf(str);
        System.out.println("integer1 = " + integer1);
        
        // Integer -> int
        int intValue = integer1.intValue();
        System.out.println("intValue = " + intValue);
        
        // int -> Integer
        Integer integer2 = Integer.valueOf(intValue);
        System.out.println("integer2 = " + integer2);
    }
}

   }

//문자열의 양쪽 공백 제거해보기
public class StringTest02 {
   
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      
      String original = "     Hello Java    ";
      
      System.out.println("앞 뒤 공백 제거 : " + original.strip());
      
      System.out.println("앞 공백 제거 : " + original.stripLeading());
      System.out.println("뒷 공백 제거 : " + original.stripTrailing());
      
   }

}

public class Example {
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      /*
      String str = "";
      for(int i = 1; i<=100;i++) {
         str +=i;
      }
      System.out.println(str);
      */
      StringBuffer sb = new StringBuffer();
      for(int i = 1;i<=100;i++) {
         sb.append(i);
      }
      String str = sb.toString();
      System.out.println(str);
   }
}

//String Buffer와 String Builder활용해서 효율적으로 만들어보기
public class Example01 {

   public static void main(String[] args) {
      /*
      String str="";
      for(int i=1; i<=100; i++) {
         str+=i;
      }
      System.out.println(str);
      */
      
      StringBuffer sb = new StringBuffer();
      for(int i = 0; i<=100; i++) {
         sb.append(i);
      }
      System.out.println(sb.toString());
   }
}

[김승우] [오전 11:41] public class Example01 {
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      /*
      String str = "";
       * for (int i = 0; i <=100; i++) { str += i; }//this is 메모리 박살 //
       */
      // 위 코드를 더 효과적으로 만드시오.
      // StringBuilder와 StringBuffer의 가장 큰 차이는 thread Safety이며, 성능 상의 큰 차이는 없다. Buffer 사용을 권장한다.
      StringBuffer sb = new StringBuffer();
      for (int i = 0; i <= 100; i++) {
         sb.append(i);
      }
      System.out.println(sb);
   }
}
[배건희] [오후 12:47] package chapter16;



public class BoxMain3 {
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      //타입 인자로 기본 타입 사용 불가
      //GenericBox<int> intBox = new GenericBox<T>();
      GenericBox<Integer> integerBox = new GenericBox<Integer>();
      integerBox.set(10);
      //integerBox.set("10");
      Integer integer = integerBox.get();
      System.out.println(integer);
      GenericBox<String> stringBox = new GenericBox<String>();
      stringBox.set("hello");
      GenericBox<Double> doubleBox = new GenericBox<Double>();
      doubleBox.set(1.12354);
      System.out.println(stringBox.get());
      System.out.println(doubleBox.get());
   }
}

[김상훈] [오후 12:48] package chapter16;

public class BoxMain3 {

   public static void main(String[] args) {
      //타입인자로는 기본타입 사용 불가
      //GenericBox<int> intBox = new GenericBox<T>();
      
      GenericBox<Integer> integerBox = new GenericBox<Integer>();
      integerBox.set(10);
      //integerBox.set("문자열 100");
      Integer integer=integerBox.get();
      System.out.println(integer);
      
      //String
      GenericBox<String> st = new GenericBox<String>();
      st.set("hello");
      String a= st.get();
      System.out.println(a);
      
      //Double
      GenericBox<Double> d = new GenericBox<Double>();
      d.set(22.2);
      double b = d.get();
      System.out.println(b);
      
   }
}

public class BoxMain3 {

   public static void main(String[] args) {
      
      // 타입인자로 기본타입 사용 불가
      // GenericBox<int> intBox = new GenericBox<T>();
      
      GenericBox<Integer> integerBox = new GenericBox<Integer>();
      integerBox.set(10);
      // integerBox.set("문자열100");
      Integer integer = integerBox.get();
      System.out.println(integer);
      
      // String
      GenericBox<String> stringBox = new GenericBox<String>();
      stringBox.set("문자열");
      String string = stringBox.get();
      System.out.println(string);
      
      // Double
      GenericBox<Double> doubleBox = new GenericBox<Double>();
      doubleBox.set(2.5);
      double db = doubleBox.get();
      System.out.println(db);

   }

public class ContainerTest {
   
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      
      Container<String> stringContainer = new Container<>();
      System.out.println("빈 값 확인 1 : " + stringContainer.isEmpty());
      
      stringContainer.setItem("data1");
      System.out.println("저장 데이터 : "+ stringContainer.getItem());
      System.out.println("빈 값 확인 2 : "  +  stringContainer.isEmpty());
      
      Container<Integer> integerContainer = new Container<>();
      integerContainer.setItem(10);
      System.out.println("저장 데이터 : "+ integerContainer.getItem());
   }

}

[배건희] [오후 3:04] package chapter16;

public class Container <T>{
   T Item;

   T getItem() {
      return Item;
   }

   void setItem(T item) {
      Item = item;
   }
   boolean isEmpty() {
      if(Item==null) {
         return true;
      }
      if(Item=="") {
         return true;
      }
      
      return false;
   }
   
   
}

}

public class Container<T> {
   
   private T value;
   
   public T getItem() {
      return value;
   }

   public void setItem(T value) {
      this.value = value;
   }

   public boolean isEmpty() {
      if(value == null) {
         return true;
      }else if(value != null) {
         return false;
      }
      return false;
   }
}

[정세나] [오후 4:36] package chapter16;

public class AnimalHostpitalMainV1 {

   public static void main(String[] args) {
      
      AnimalHostpitalV1 dogHospital = new AnimalHostpitalV1();
      AnimalHostpitalV1 catHospital = new AnimalHostpitalV1();
      
      Dog dog = new Dog("멍멍이1", 100);
      Cat cat = new Cat("냐옹이1", 300);
      
      //강아지 병원
      dogHospital.set(dog);
      dogHospital.checkup();
      
      //고양이 병원
      catHospital.set(cat);
      catHospital.checkup();
      
      //문제1: 강아지병원에 고양이 전달(컴파일 오류 발생하지 않음)
      dogHospital.set(cat);
      
      //문제2 : 캐스팅 문제
      dogHospital.set(dog);
       Dog biggerDog = (Dog)dogHospital.bigger(new Dog("멍멍이2", 200));
       System.out.println(biggerDog);
       
      
   }

}

[김승우] [오후 4:49] package chapter16;

public class Pair<T1, T2> {
   private T1 first;
   private T2 second;

   public T1 getFirst() {return first;}
   public void setFirst(T1 first) {this.first = first;}
   public T2 getSecond() {return second;}
   public void setSecond(T2 second) {this.second = second;}
   @Override
   public String toString() {
      return this.getClass().getSimpleName() + "의 first는 " + first + ", second는 " + second;
   }
}

[김진용] [오후 12:19] package chapter17;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.Scanner;

public class PersonManager {

   //선언
      private ArrayList<Person> arrayList;
      
      public PersonManager() {
         arrayList = new ArrayList<Person>();
      }
      
      //저장
      public void addPerson(Person person) {
            System.out.println("-----정보추가-----");
            System.out.print("이름 : ");
            Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
            
            Person ui = new Person();
            ui.setName(sc.next());
            
            System.out.print("나이 : ");
            ui.setAge(sc.nextInt());
            
            System.out.print("전화 : ");
            ui.setTel(sc.next());
            
            arrayList.add(ui);
            System.out.println("정보가 저장되었습니다.");
            System.out.println("---------------------------------");
         
      }
      //삭제
      public boolean removePerson(String name) {
         Iterator<Person> it = arrayList.iterator();
         
         while(it.hasNext()) {
            Person person = it.next();
            String personId = person.getName();
            if(personId.equals(name)) {
               arrayList.remove(person);
               System.out.println(name+"의 정보를 삭제했습니다.");
               return true;
            }
         }
         System.out.println(name+"가 존재하지 않습니다.");
         return false;
      }
      
      //조회
      public void showAllPerson() {
         System.out.println("--------전체정보--------");
         for(Person person : arrayList) {
            System.out.println("이름 : "+person.getName());
            System.out.println("나이 : "+person.getAge());
            System.out.println("번호 : "+person.getTel());
            System.out.println("---------------------");
         }
         System.out.println();
      }

      public void personMgr() {
         boolean a = true;
         Scanner scan = new Scanner(System.in);
         while(a) {
            System.out.println("1. 회원추가");
            System.out.println("2. 회원탈퇴");
            System.out.println("3. 회원정보");
            System.out.println("4. 종료");
            System.out.print("항목선택 : ");
            int num = scan.nextInt();
            switch (num) {
            case 1:
               addPerson(null);
               break;
            case 2:
               System.out.print("삭제할 이름 : ");
               removePerson(scan.next());
               break;
            case 3:
               showAllPerson();
               break;
            case 4:
               a = false;
               break;

            default:
               break;
            }
         }
         
         
      }
   
   
   
}

[김승우] [오후 12:22] import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Scanner;

public class PersonManager {
   public void personMgr() {
      Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
      List<Person> personList = new ArrayList<>();
      boolean run = true, deleted = false;
      String input;
      while (run) {
         showMenu();
         input = sc.nextLine();
         switch (input) {
         case "1":
            Person newPerson = new Person();
            System.out.println("-----정보추가-----");
            System.out.print("이름 : ");
            newPerson.setName(sc.nextLine());
            System.out.print("나이 : ");
            newPerson.setAge(Integer.parseInt(sc.nextLine()));
            System.out.print("전화 : ");
            newPerson.setTel(sc.nextLine());
            personList.add(newPerson);
            System.out.println("정보가 저장되었습니다.");
            System.out.println("---------------------------------");
            break;
         case "2":
            System.out.println("-----정보삭제-----");
            System.out.print("삭제할 이름 : ");
            input = sc.nextLine();
            for (Person person : personList) {
               if (person.getName().equals(input)) {
                  personList.remove(person);
                  System.out.println(input + "의 정보를 삭제했습니다.");
                  deleted = true;
                  break;
               }
            }
            if (!deleted)
               System.out.println(input + "이 존재하지 않습니다.");
            break;
         case "3":
            System.out.println("--------전체정보--------");
            System.out.printf("등록인원 %d명\n", personList.size());
            for (Person person : personList) {
               System.out.println("이름 : " + person.getName());
               System.out.println("나이 : " + person.getAge());
               System.out.println("번호 : " + person.getTel());
               System.out.println("---------------------");
            }
            break;
         case "4":
            System.out.println("프로그램 종료");
            run = false;
            break;
         default:
            System.out.println("존재하지 않는 메뉴입니다.");
            break;
         }
      }

      sc.close();
   }

   private void showMenu() {
      System.out.print("1. 회원추가\r\n" + "2. 회원탈퇴\r\n" + "3. 회원정보\r\n" + "4. 종  료\r\n" + "항목선택 : ");
   }
}
[배건희] [오후 12:23] package chapter17;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.Scanner;

public class PersonManager {
   Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
   ArrayList<Person> arr = new ArrayList<Person>();
   
   private boolean on = true;
   public void personMgr() {
      while(on) {
         showSelection();
         switch(Integer.parseInt(sc.next())) {
         case 1:
            System.out.println("-------정보 추가-------");
            System.out.print("이름 : ");
            String newName=sc.next();
            System.out.print("나이 : ");
            int newAge=Integer.parseInt(sc.next());
            System.out.print("전화번호 : ");
            String newTel=sc.next();
            arr.add(new Person(newName,newAge,newTel));
            System.out.println("정보가 저장되었습니다.");
            break;
         case 2:
            System.out.println("-------정보 삭제-------");
            System.out.print("삭제할 이름 : ");
            removeUser(sc.next());
            break;
         case 3:
            System.out.println("-------전체 정보-------");
            showAllUser();
            break;
         case 4:
            killSys();
            break;
         default :
            System.out.println("잘못된 입력입니다.");
            break;
         }
      }
   }
   private boolean removeUser(String delName) {
      Iterator<Person> it = arr.iterator();
      while(it.hasNext()) {
         Person tempP = it.next();
         if(delName.equals(tempP.getName())) {
            arr.remove(tempP);
            System.out.println(tempP.getName()+"의 정보를 삭제했습니다.");
            return true;
         }
      }
      System.out.println(delName+"의 정보가 존재하지 않습니다.");
      return false;
      
   }
   private void showAllUser() {
      System.out.println("등록인원 "+arr.size()+"명");
      for(Person p:arr) {
         System.out.println(p);
         System.out.println("-------------");
      }
   }
   private void killSys() {
      on=false;
   }
   private void showSelection() {
      System.out.println("1.회원 추가");
      System.out.println("2.회원 탈퇴");
      System.out.println("3.회원 정보");
      System.out.println("4.종료");
      System.out.print("항목 선택 : ");
   }
}

[김도영] [오후 12:39] 삭제된 메시지입니다.
[김도영] [오후 12:42] package Chapter17;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.Scanner;

public class PersonManager {

   private ArrayList<Person> arrayList;
   
   public PersonManager() {
      arrayList = new ArrayList<Person>();
   }
   
   public void addPerson() {
      Person person = new Person();
      Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
      System.out.println("-----정보추가-----");
      System.out.print("이름 : ");
      String name = sc.next();
      person.setName(name);
      System.out.print("나이 : ");
      int age = sc.nextInt();
      person.setAge(age);
      System.out.print("전화 : ");
      String tel = sc.next();
      person.setTel(tel);
      arrayList.add(person);
      System.out.println("정보가 저장되었습니다");
   }
   
   public boolean removePerson() {
      Iterator<Person> it = arrayList.iterator();
      System.out.print("삭제할 이름 : ");
      Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
      String name = sc.next();
      
      while(it.hasNext()) {
         Person person = it.next();
         String personName = person.getName();
         if(personName.equals(name)) {
            arrayList.remove(person);
            System.out.println(name + "의 정보를 삭제했습니다");
            return true;
         }
      }
      System.out.println(name + "이 존재하지 않습니다.");
      return false;
   }
   
   public void infoPerson() {
      System.out.println("--------전체정보--------");
      int num = arrayList.size();
      System.out.println("등록인원 " + num + "명");
      for (int i=0; i<arrayList.size(); i++) { 
         System.out.println("이름 : " + arrayList.get(i).getName());
         System.out.println("나이 : " + arrayList.get(i).getAge());
         System.out.println("번호 : " + arrayList.get(i).getTel());
         System.out.println("---------------------");
      }
   }
   
   
   public void personMgr() {
      Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
      
      while(true) {
         System.out.println("1. 회원추가");
         System.out.println("2. 회원탈퇴");
         System.out.println("3. 회원정보");
         System.out.println("4. 종 료");
         System.out.print("항목선택 : ");
         int num = sc.nextInt();
         if (num == 1) {
            addPerson();
            System.out.println("---------------------");
         }else if(num == 2) {
            removePerson();
            System.out.println("---------------------");
         }else if(num == 3) {
            infoPerson();
         }else if(num == 4) {
            System.out.println("프로그램 종료");
            break;
         }else {
            System.out.println("잘못된 번호입니다.");
         }
      }
      sc.close();
   }
}

[강지훈] [오후 12:52] package chapter17;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.Scanner;

public class PersonManager {
   Scanner sc= new Scanner(System.in);
   
   int k;
   ArrayList<Person> al = new ArrayList<Person>();
   
   public void personMgr() {
      
      
      while(true) {
      System.out.println("1. 회원추가");
      System.out.println("2. 회원탈퇴");
      System.out.println("3. 회원정보");
      System.out.println("4. 종  료");
      System.out.print("항목선택 : ");
      int k =sc.nextInt();
      

      
      
      if(k == 1) {
         Person ps = new Person();
         System.out.print("이름 : ");
         ps.setName(sc.next());
         System.out.print("나이 : ");
         ps.setAge(sc.nextInt());
         System.out.print("전화 : ");
         ps.setTel(sc.next());
         al.add(ps);
      }
      
      else if(k == 2) {
          System.out.println("삭제할 이름 : ");
          String name = sc.next();

          boolean found = false;
          for (int i = 0; i < al.size(); i++) {
              Person p = al.get(i);  
              if (p.getName().equals(name)) {
                  al.remove(i);  
                  System.out.println(name + "의 정보를 삭제했습니다.");
                  found = true;
                  break; 
              }
          }

          if (!found) {
              System.out.println("해당 이름을 가진 회원이 없습니다.");
          }
      }
         
      
      else if(k==3) {
         
         System.out.println("등록인원 : "+al.size()+"명");
         for(int i=0;i<al.size();i++) {
            System.out.println("이름 : "+al.get(i).getName());
            System.out.println("나이 : "+al.get(i).getAge());
            System.out.println("전화 : "+al.get(i).getTel());
         }
         
      }
      else if (k==4) {
         System.out.println("프로그램 종료");
         break;
         
      }
      
      }
   
   }
   
}

[정세나] [오후 1:05] package chapter17;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.Scanner;

public class PersonManager {
   
   public void personMgr() {
      
      ArrayList<Person> personArr = new ArrayList<Person>();
      Scanner scan = new Scanner(System.in);
      while(true) {
         System.out.println("1. 회원추가");
         System.out.println("2. 회원탈퇴");
         System.out.println("3. 회원정보");
         System.out.println("4. 종 료 ");
         System.out.print("항목 선택 : ");
         
         int select = scan.nextInt();
         
         switch (select) {
         case 1:
            Person p = new Person();
            System.out.println("----정보 추가-----");
            
            System.out.print("이름 : ");
            p.setName(scan.next());
            
            System.out.print("나이 : ");
            p.setAge(scan.nextInt());
            
            System.out.print("전화 : ");
            p.setTel(scan.next());
            
            personArr.add(p);
            System.out.println("정보가 저장되었습니다.");
            System.out.println("----------------------------------------");
            break;
         case 2:
            System.out.println("-----정보 삭제-----");
            System.out.print("삭제할 이름 : ");
            String name = scan.next();
            for(int i = 0 ; i < personArr.size(); i++) {
               if(personArr.get(i).getName().equals(name)) {
                  personArr.remove(i);
                  System.out.println(name + "의 정보를 삭제했습니다.");
                  break;
               }else {
                  if (i+1 == personArr.size())
                     System.out.println(name + " 이 존재하지 않습니다.");
               }
            }
            break;
         case 3:
            System.out.println("-----전체정보-----");
            System.out.println("등록 인원 " + personArr.size() + "명");
            /*
            for(int i = 0 ; i < personArr.size(); i++) {
               System.out.println("이름 : " + personArr.get(i).getName());
               System.out.println("나이 : " + personArr.get(i).getAge());
               System.out.println("번호 : " + personArr.get(i).getTel());
               System.out.println("--------------------------");
            }
            */
            Iterator<Person> it =personArr.iterator();
            while(it.hasNext()) {
               Person currentPerson = it.next();
               System.out.println("이름 : " + currentPerson.getName());
               System.out.println("나이 : " + currentPerson.getAge());
               System.out.println("번호 : " + currentPerson.getTel());
               System.out.println("--------------------------");
            }
            break;
         default:
            System.out.println("프로그램 종료");
            return;
         }
      }
   }
   
}

[배건희] [오후 2:46] package chapter17;

import java.util.ArrayList;

public class ArrayEx1 {
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      ArrayList<Integer> arr = new ArrayList<>();
      arr.add(90);
      arr.add(80);
      arr.add(70);
      arr.add(60);
      arr.add(50);
      int total = 0;
      for(Integer now:arr) {
         total+=now;
      }
      double average=(double)total/arr.size();
      System.out.println("점수 총합"+total);
      System.out.println("점수 평균"+average);
      
   }
}

[김혁진] [오후 2:46] package chapter17;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

public class ArrayEx1 {

   public static void main(String[] args) {
      
      List<Integer> list = new ArrayList<Integer>();
      list.add(90);
      list.add(80);
      list.add(70);
      list.add(60);
      list.add(50);
      
      int total = 0;
      for(int score : list) {
         total += score;
      }
      
      System.out.println("점수 총합 : " + total);
      System.out.println("점수 평균 : " + (double)total / list.size());
   }
   
}

[김승우] [오후 2:47] public class ArrayEx1 {
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      int total;
      double avg;

      List<Integer> ls = new ArrayList<>();
      for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
         ls.add(50 + i * 10);
      }
      total = 0;
      for (Integer i : ls) {
         total += i;
      }
      avg = (double) total / ls.size();
      System.out.println("total >> " + total);
      System.out.println("avg >> " + avg);
   }
}
[김진용] [오후 2:48] package chapter17;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.List;

//리스트를  사용해서 바꿔보세요!
public class ArrayEx1 {

   public static void main(String[] args) {
      
//      int[] students = {90,80,70,60,50};
//      
//      int total = 0;
//      for(int i=0;i<students.length;i++) {
//         total += students[i];
//      }
//      double average = (double)total/students.length;
//      System.out.println("점수 총합 : "+total);
//      System.out.println("점수 평균 : "+average);
      
      List<Integer> students = new ArrayList<Integer>();
      int total = 0;
      students.add(90);
      students.add(80);
      students.add(70);
      students.add(60);
      students.add(50);
      
      Iterator<Integer> it = students.iterator();
      while(it.hasNext()) {
         total += it.next();
      }
      double average = (double)total/students.size();
      System.out.println("점수 총합 : "+total);
      System.out.println("점수 평균 : "+average);
   }

}

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

public class ArrayEx1 {
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      /*
      int[] students= {90,80,70,60,50};
      
      int total=0;
      for(int i = 0 ; i<students.length;i++) {
         total += students[i];
      }
      
      double avg = (double)total / students.length;
      System.out.println("점수 총합 : " + total);
      System.out.println("점수 평균 : " + avg);
      */
      
      List<Integer> list = new ArrayList<Integer>();
      
      list.add(90);
      list.add(80);
      list.add(70);
      list.add(60);
      list.add(50);
      
      int sum=0;
      float avg;
      
      for(int i =0;i<list.size();i++) {
         int k = list.get(i);
         sum +=k;
      }
      avg = sum/list.size();
      System.out.println("점수 총합 : " +sum);
      System.out.println("점수 평균 : " + avg);
      
   }

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

public class ArrayEx1 {

   public static void main(String[] args) {

      int[] students = {90, 80, 70, 60, 50};

      List<Integer> li = new ArrayList<Integer>();
      li.add(90);
      li.add(80);
      li.add(70);
      li.add(60);
      li.add(50);
      
      int total = 0;
      for(int score : li ) {
         total += score;
      }
      
      System.out.println("점수 총합 : " + total);
      System.out.println("점수 평균 : " + (double)total / li.size());
   }

}

[기범준] [오후 2:54] package Chapter17;

import java.util.ArrayList;

public class ArrayEx1 {

   public static void main(String[] args) {

      ArrayList<Integer> num = new ArrayList<Integer>();
      num.add(90);
      num.add(80);
      num.add(70);
      num.add(60);
      num.add(50);
      int total = 0;
      
      
      for(int i=0; i<num.size(); i++) {
         total += num.get(i);
      }
      
      double average = (double)total/num.size();
      System.out.println("점수 총합 : "+total);
      System.out.println("점수 평균 : "+average);
      
   }

}

[정세나] [오후 3:32]   Object item;   
    Node next;

    public Node(Object item) {
        this.item = item;
    }

    
    //반복문 안에서 문자를 더하기 때문에 StringBuilder사용
    @Override
    public String toString() {
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        Node x = this;
        sb.append("[");
        while (x != null) {
            sb.append(x.item);
            if (x.next != null) {
                sb.append("->");
            }
            x = x.next;
        }
        sb.append("]");
        return sb.toString();
    }
[정세나] [오후 3:32]     private Node first;   
    private int size = 0;

    public void add(Object e) {
        Node newNode = new Node(e);
        if (first == null) {
            first = newNode;
        } else {
            Node lastNode = getLastNode();
            lastNode.next = newNode;
        }
        size++;
    }

    private Node getLastNode() {
        Node x = first;
        while (x.next != null) {
            x = x.next;
        }
        return x;
    }

    public Object set(int index, Object element) {
        Node x = getNode(index);
        Object oldValue = x.item;
        x.item = element;
        return oldValue;
    }

    public Object get(int index) {
        Node node = getNode(index);
        return node.item;
    }

    private Node getNode(int index) {
        Node x = first;
        for (int i = 0; i < index; i++) {
            x = x.next;
        }
        return x;
    }

    public int indexOf(Object o) {
        int index = 0;
        for (Node x = first; x != null; x = x.next) {
            if (o.equals(x.item))
                return index;
            index++;
        }
        return -1;
    }

    public int size() {
        return size;
    }

    
    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "MyLinkedListV1{" +
                "first=" + first +
                ", size=" + size +
                "}";
    }
[정세나] [오후 4:07] package chapter17;


import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.LinkedList;

public class MemberLinkedList {

   // 선언
   private LinkedList<Member> linkedList;

   public MemberLinkedList() {
      linkedList = new LinkedList<Member>();
      }

   // 저장
   public void addMember(Member member) {
      linkedList.add(member);
   }

   // 삭제
   public boolean removeMember(int memberId) {
      Iterator<Member> it = linkedList.iterator();

      while (it.hasNext()) {
         Member member = it.next();
         int tempId = member.getMemberId();
         if (tempId == memberId) {
            linkedList.remove(member);
            return true;
         }
      }
      System.out.println(memberId + "가 존재하지 않습니다");
      return false;
   }

   // 조회
   public void showAllMember() {
      for (Member member : linkedList) {
         System.out.println(member);
      }
      System.out.println();
   }

}

[정세나] [오후 4:35] package chapter17;

public class Item {
   
   private String name;
   private int price;
   private int quantity;
   
   
   public Item(String name, int price, int quantity) {
      this.name = name;
      this.price = price;
      this.quantity = quantity;
   }
   
   public String getName() {
      return name;
   }
   
   public int getTotalPrice() {
      return price * quantity;
   }
   

}

[배건희] [오후 4:44] package chapter17;

import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.LinkedList;

public class ShoppingCart {
   LinkedList<Item> cart = new LinkedList<Item>();
   public void addItem(Item item) {
      cart.add(item);
      
   }
   public void displayItem() {
      Iterator<Item> it = cart.iterator();
      int totalCartTotalPrice = 0;
      for(Item item:cart) {
         System.out.printf("상품명 : %s, 합계 : %d\n",item.getName(),item.getTotalPrice());
         totalCartTotalPrice+=it.next().getTotalPrice();
      }
      System.out.printf("전체 가격 합 : %d\n",totalCartTotalPrice);
   }
}

import java.util.Iterator;

//중복값을 제거하고 값을 출력하쇼
//{30,20,20,10,10}
public class SetTest {
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      int[] arr = { 30, 20, 20, 10, 10 };
      Set<Integer> set = new HashSet<>();
      for (int i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
         set.add(arr[i]);
      }
      Iterator<Integer> iter = set.iterator();
      while (iter.hasNext()) {
         System.out.println(iter.next());
      }
   }
}

import java.util.Set;

public class SetTest {

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        
        Integer[] inputArr = {30, 20, 20, 10, 10};
        
        // HashSet을 사용해 중복 값을 제거
        Set<Integer> set = new HashSet<>();
        
        for (Integer num : inputArr) {
            set.add(num);
        }
        
        // 출력 순서를 상관하지 않음
        for (Integer num : set) {
            System.out.println(num);
        }
    }

[김동후] [오전 10:57] package chapter18;

import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.Set;

//중복 값을 제거하고 값을 출력

//실행결과
//20
//10
//30
public class SetTest {

   public static void main(String[] args) {
      Integer[] inputArr = {30,20,20,10,10};

      Set<Integer> integer = new HashSet<>();
      for(int i = 0; i<inputArr.length; i++) {
         integer.add(inputArr[i]);
      }
      Iterator<Integer> it= integer.iterator();
         while(it.hasNext()) {
            System.out.println(it.next());
         }
   }
}
[김현준] [오전 10:58] package chapter18;

import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.Set;

//중복 값을 제거하고 값을 출력해보기 (순서는 상관없다.)
/*
실행결과
20
10
30
*/
public class SetTest01 {
   
   public static void main(String[] args) {
      
      Integer[] inputArr = { 30, 20, 20, 10, 10 };
      
      Set<Integer> set = new HashSet<Integer>();
      
      for(Integer num:inputArr) {       //새로 만든 함수값인 num 값을 set에 삽입하기
         set.add(num);
      }
      
      for(Integer num:set) {             //set 으로 중복을 없앤 처리를 위에서 실행했으므로 set 을 출력해주는 게 맞다.   
         System.out.println(num);
      }  
   }
}
